    "\n",
    "%matplotlib inline\n",
    "mat_contents=sio.loadmat('Case2-2.mat')\n",
    "c = mat_contents['Freq_domain']\n",
    "d = mat_contents['Hf_chan_2']\n",
    "H= (20)*(np.log10(np.abs(d)))\n",
    "plt.plot(c,H)\n",
    "plt.grid('on')\n",
    "plt.xlabel('$Freq,Hz$')\n",
    "plt.ylabel('$H,dB$')\n",
    "plt.title('$Magn$ versus $Freq$')\n",
